ä»¥ä¸‹ã®é››å½¢ã‚’è²¼ã‚Šä»˜ã‘ï¼š

#!/usr/bin/env python3

import yaml
import sys
import time

CONFIG = "consensus_weights.yaml"

def load_config():
    with open(CONFIG, 'r') as f:
        return yaml.safe_load(f)

def collect_votes():
    # ãƒ€ãƒŸãƒ¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼ˆå®Ÿé‹ç”¨ã§ã¯å®Ÿéš›ã®Botå¿œç­”ã¨ç½®ãæ›ãˆï¼‰
    return {
        'Nancy_Architect': 'approve',
        'Nancy_VPS_Engineer': 'approve',
        'Nancy_GitHub': 'reject',
        'BirdBot_GitHub_Inspector': 'approve',
        'BirdBot_VPS_Inspector': 'approve',
        'DogBot_Guard': 'reject',
    }

def calculate_consensus(votes, weights):
    score = {}
    for bot, vote in votes.items():
        weight = weights.get(bot, 1)
        score[vote] = score.get(vote, 0) + weight
    return max(score.items(), key=lambda x: x[1])

def main():
    config = load_config()
    weights = config['weights']
    fallback = config['fallback_decider']

    print("â³ æŠ•ç¥¨ã‚’é›†è¨ˆä¸­â€¦")
    start = time.time()
    votes = collect_votes()
    elapsed = time.time() - start

    if elapsed > config['timeout_seconds']:
        print(f"âš ï¸ ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ ã‚¢ã‚¦ãƒˆã€‚{fallback} ã«æ±ºå®šæ¨©ã‚’å§”è­²ã—ã¾ã™ã€‚")
        sys.exit(0)

    decision, score = calculate_consensus(votes, weights)
    print(f"âœ… Consensusæ±ºå®š: {decision}ï¼ˆã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢: {score}ï¼‰")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

ã‚‚ã— vps_watcher.py ã«ãƒ­ã‚°è¨­å®šãŒç„¡ã„ãƒ»ä¸å®Œå…¨ã§ã‚ã‚Œã°ã€ä»¥ä¸‹ã®ã‚ˆã†ã«ä¿®æ­£ã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

import os
import time
import psutil
import logging

log_path = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '../logs/vps_watcher.log')
logging.basicConfig(filename=log_path, level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s %(message)s')

def monitor():
    while True:
        cpu = psutil.cpu_percent(interval=1)
        mem = psutil.virtual_memory().percent
        logging.info(f"CPU: {cpu}%, MEM: {mem}%")
        time.sleep(5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    monitor()

#!/usr/bin/env python3

import os
import datetime
import shutil
import psutil

LOG_FILE = "/home/nancyuser/tamajinja-project/logs/vps_watcher.log"
now = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("[%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S]")

def log(msg):
    with open(LOG_FILE, "a") as f:
        f.write(f"{now} {msg}\n")

# CPU load
load1, load5, load15 = os.getloadavg()
log(f"CPU Load avg (1/5/15 min): {load1:.2f} / {load5:.2f} / {load15:.2f}")

# Memory usage
mem = psutil.virtual_memory()
log(f"Memory: {mem.percent}% used")

# Disk usage
disk = shutil.disk_usage("/")
disk_used_percent = (disk.used / disk.total) * 100
log(f"Disk: {disk_used_percent:.2f}% used")

ğŸª„ ä¿®æ­£ç‰ˆã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆ
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import os
import datetime
import shutil
import psutil
import time

LOG_FILE = "/home/nancyuser/tamajinja-project/nancy/logs/vps_watcher.log"

def log(msg):
    now = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("[%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S]")
    with open(LOG_FILE, "a") as f:
        f.write(f"{now} {msg}\n")

def monitor():
    while True:
        # CPU load
        load1, load5, load15 = os.getloadavg()
        log(f"CPU Load avg (1/5/15 min): {load1:.2f} / {load5:.2f} / {load15:.2f}")

        # Memory usage
        mem = psutil.virtual_memory()
        log(f"Memory: {mem.percent}% used")

        # Disk usage
        disk = shutil.disk_usage("/")
        disk_used_percent = (disk.used / disk.total) * 100
        log(f"Disk: {disk_used_percent:.2f}% used")

        time.sleep(5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    monitor()

# Each task to run has to be defined through a single line

import os
import time

log_file = "/home/nancyuser/tamajinja-project/nancy/logs/vps_watcher.log"
days_to_keep = 7
cutoff = time.time() - days_to_keep * 86400

with open(log_file, "r") as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

with open(log_file, "w") as f:
    for line in lines:
        timestamp = line.split("]")[0].strip("[").split("T")[0]
        log_time = time.mktime(time.strptime(timestamp, "%Y-%m-%d"))
        if log_time >= cutoff:
            f.write(line)

import os
import psutil
import datetime

def log_resource_usage():
    now = datetime.datetime.now().isoformat(timespec='seconds')
    cpu = psutil.getloadavg()
    mem = psutil.virtual_memory().percent
    disk = psutil.disk_usage('/').percent
    log = f"[{now}] CPU Load avg (1/5/15 min): {cpu[0]:.2f} / {cpu[1]:.2f} / {cpu[2]:.2f}\n" \
          f"[{now}] Memory: {mem:.1f}% used\n" \
          f"[{now}] Disk: {disk:.2f}% used\n"
    with open('/home/nancyuser/tamajinja-project/nancy/logs/vps_watcher.log', 'a') as f:
        f.write(log)

def monitor():
    log_resource_usage()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    monitor()

# Edit this file to introduce tasks to be run by cron.
# 
# Each task to run has to be defined through a single line
# indicating with different fields when the task will be run
# and what command to run for the task
# 
# To define the time you can provide concrete values for
# minute (m), hour (h), day of month (dom), month (mon),
# and day of week (dow) or use '*' in these fields (for 'any').
# 
# Notice that tasks will be started based on the cron's system
# daemon's notion of time and timezones.
# 
# Output of the crontab jobs (including errors) is sent through
# email to the user the crontab file belongs to (unless redirected).
# 
# For example, you can run a backup of all your user accounts
# at 5 a.m every week with:
# 0 5 * * 1 tar -zcf /var/backups/home.tgz /home/
# 
# For more information see the manual pages of crontab(5) and cron(8)
# 
# m h  dom mon dow   command
